<h3>How to download and unpack files</h3>
<div class="clear"></div><div class="divider divider-normal" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"></div>
<div style="font-size: 9pt;">Clicking any of the links above will get you to download page from various file-locker services where you can download file for free.</div>
<div class="clear"></div><div class="divider divider-normal" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"></div>
<div style="font-size: 9pt;">Downloaded files are archived in .rar format with password that is always <span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>hef</strong></span>. Use free <span style="color: #800000;"><em><strong><a href="https://www.7-zip.org/" rel="noopener" style="color: #800000;" target="_blank">7zip</a></strong></em></span> winarchiver to unpack files.</div>
<div class="clear"></div><div class="divider divider-normal" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"></div>
<div style="font-size: 9pt;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>If you get error</strong></span> while unpacking similar to this.</div>
<div><span style="color: #333399; font-size: 9pt;"> xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx</span></div>
<div><span style="color: #333399; font-size: 9pt;">security data</span><br/>
<span style="color: #333399; font-size: 9pt;">! This security ID may not be assigned as the owner of this object.</span></div>
<div style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"></div>
<div style="font-size: 9pt;"><strong>Don’t break the proces! File will unpack</strong>. This is because I use various win rar versions in the past. Use the latest 7zip or WinRar archiver.</div>
<div class="clear"></div><div class="divider divider-normal" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"></div>
